    OnPreReport=BEGIN

                  IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                    CREATE(xlApp,FALSE,TRUE);

                    xlSheet.Select;
                    Language := xlApp.LanguageSettings.LanguageID(1);
                    xlSheet.Range('A6:U5000').Font.Name := 'Arial';
                    xlSheet.Range('A6:U5000').Font.Size := 8;
                    xlSheet.Range('A6:U7').Font.Bold := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('A6:U7').HorizontalAlignment := 2;
                    xlApp.Range('A8').Select;
                    xlApp.ActiveWindow.FreezePanes := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('A7:U5000').AutoFilter;

                    xlSheet.Range('A1').Value := 'Status Projectmaterialen';
                    xlSheet.Range('A1').Font.Bold := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('A1').Font.Size := 12;

                    xlSheet.Range('A2').Value := COMPANYNAME;
                    IF Job.GETFILTER("No.") <> '' THEN
                      xlSheet.Range('A4').Value := STRSUBSTNO('Projectfilter: %1',Job.GETFILTER("No."));
                    IF "Budget Line".GETFILTER(Element) <>'' THEN
                      xlSheet.Range('A5').Value := STRSUBSTNO('Elementfilter: %1',"Budget Line".GETFILTER(Element));

                    //Headers
                    xlSheet.Range('A6:D6').Merge;
                    xlSheet.Range('A6:D6')._BorderAround(1);
                    xlSheet.Range('E6:F6').Merge;
                    xlSheet.Range('E6:F6')._BorderAround(1);
                    xlSheet.Range('G6:I6').Merge;
                    xlSheet.Range('G6:I6')._BorderAround(1);
                    xlSheet.Range('J6:L6').Merge;

                    xlSheet.Range('M6:O6').Merge;
                    xlSheet.Range('M6:O6')._BorderAround(1);
                    xlSheet.Range('P6:Q6').Merge;
                    xlSheet.Range('P6:Q6')._BorderAround(1);
                    xlSheet.Range('R6:S6').Merge;
                    xlSheet.Range('R6:S6')._BorderAround(1);
                    xlSheet.Range('T6:U6').Merge;
                    xlSheet.Range('T6:U6')._BorderAround(1);

                    RowNo := 6;
                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 21 DO BEGIN
                      CellCde[ColNo] := Matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                    END;

                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := 'Project structuur';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := 'Artikel gegevens';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := 'Begroot';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Adviesorder status';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := 'Logistiek';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := 'Leverdata';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := 'Ontvangststatus';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := 'Projectvoorraad';
                    RowNo += 1;

                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 21 DO BEGIN
                      CellCde[ColNo] := Matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                    END;
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := 'Projectnr';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := 'Element';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := 'Begindatum';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := 'Omschrijving';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := 'Artikel nr.';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := 'Omschrijving';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := 'MMW contract';

                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := 'Geadviseerd';

                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := 'Verwerkt';

                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := 'Artikel dagboek';

                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := 'Toegezegd';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := 'Nog te ontvangen';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := 'Ontvangen';
                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := 'Voorraad';

                  END;

                   IF PrintToExcel THEN

                 END;

    { 1100525002;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012001;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Project No.,Element,Cost Type,Cost Object,Extension Contract Status,Version Date)
                                 WHERE(Cost Type=CONST(Material));
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               AdviceOrder@1100525001 : Record 11012055;
                               JobInventory@1100525000 : Record 11012670;
                             BEGIN

                               TempAdviceOrderLine.RESET;
                               TempAdviceOrderLine.DELETEALL;
                               CLEAR(TempAdviceOrderLine);

                               TempJobInventory.RESET;
                               TempJobInventory.DELETEALL;
                               CLEAR(TempJobInventory);

                               AdviceOrder.RESET;
                               AdviceOrder.SETRANGE("Record Type",AdviceOrder."Record Type"::Project);
                               AdviceOrder.SETRANGE("Project No.",Job."No.");
                               IF "Budget Line".GETFILTER(Element) <> '' THEN
                                 AdviceOrder.SETRANGE(Element,"Budget Line".GETFILTER(Element));
                               IF AdviceOrder.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                 REPEAT
                                   TempAdviceOrderLine := AdviceOrder;
                                   TempAdviceOrderLine.INSERT;
                                 UNTIL AdviceOrder.NEXT = 0;
                               END;

                               JobInventory.SETRANGE( "Project No."       ,  Job."No.");
                               JobInventory.SETFILTER("Inventory Quantity", '<>%1', 0);
                               IF "Budget Line".GETFILTER(Element) <> '' THEN
                                 JobInventory.SETRANGE(Element,"Budget Line".GETFILTER(Element));
                               IF JobInventory.FINDSET(FALSE, FALSE) THEN REPEAT
                                 TempJobInventory := JobInventory;
                                 TempJobInventory.INSERT(FALSE);
                               UNTIL JobInventory.NEXT = 0;

                               TempAdviceOrderLine.RESET;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  i@1100525003 : Integer;
                                  AdviceOrderLine@1100525002 : Record 11012055;
                                  PurchLine@1100525001 : Record 39;
                                  ProjElement@1100525000 : Record 11012010;
                                BEGIN

                                  ClearVariables;
                                  AdviceOrderFound := GetAdviceOrder("Project No.",Element,"Item No.",GAdvice,GProcessed,GReceived,GStatus,GPurchCode,GAskDate,
                                                      GPromDate, GQuantArtDagb, GStockQuant, GToReceive, GTransAct, GLineNo, FALSE, Description);

                                  IF NOT Advised THEN
                                    GAdviceBl := FALSE
                                  ELSE
                                    GAdviceBl := TRUE;

                                  IF (GTransAct = 'Inkoop') AND (GLineNo <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                    IF AdviceOrderLine.GET(AdviceOrderLine."Record Type"::Project,"Project No.",'',GLineNo) THEN BEGIN
                                      PurchLine.SETRANGE("Job No.","Project No.");
                                      PurchLine.SETRANGE("Purchase Route Reference",AdviceOrderLine."Purchase Route Reference");
                                      IF PurchLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                        GStockQuant := PurchLine."Outstanding Quantity";//PurchLine."Qty. to Receive";

                                        GProcessed :=  AdviceOrderLine."Quantity (Processed)"; // + PurchLine."Quantity Received";
                                        GProcessed1 := PurchLine."Quantity Received";
                                        //GProcessed := AdviceOrderLine."Quantity (Processed)";//29-10-2010.GB
                                      END;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  CLEAR(StartDate);
                                  IF Element <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF ProjElement.GET("Project No.",Element) THEN
                                      IF ProjElement."Starting Date" <> 0D THEN
                                        StartDate := ProjElement."Starting Date";
                                  END;

                                  IF (GStatus = 'Afgehandeld') AND (GTransAct = 'Voorraad') THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (GQuantArtDagb <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                      GStockQuant := GQuantArtDagb;
                                      GProcessed1 := GProcessed - GQuantArtDagb;
                                    END ELSE BEGIN

                                      GProcessed1 := GProcessed - AdviceOrderLine."Quantity (Processed)";
                                      GStockQuant := GProcessed - GProcessed1;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF (GStatus = 'Open') AND (GTransAct = 'Voorraad') THEN BEGIN
                                    GProcessed1 := 0;
                                    GStockQuant := 0;
                                  END;

                                  //FROM SECTION

                                  IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 21 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := Matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := Job."No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := Element;
                                    IF StartDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := FORMAT(StartDate);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := "Element Description";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := "Item No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := "Extension Contract";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := FORMAT(Quantity);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := FORMAT(GAdviceBl);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := FORMAT(GAdvice);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := FORMAT(GProcessed);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := FORMAT(GStatus);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := FORMAT(GQuantArtDagb);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[14]).Value := FORMAT(GTransAct);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[15]).Value := FORMAT(GPurchCode);
                                    IF GAskDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := GAskDate;
                                    IF GPromDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := GPromDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := FORMAT(GStockQuant);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := FORMAT(GProcessed1);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := FORMAT(JobStock("Item No.", Job."No.", Element));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Value := FORMAT(JobStockDelivery("Item No.", Job."No.", Element));
                                    RowNo +=1;
                                  END;

                                  ShowBL2 := (AdviceOrderFound);
                                  ShowBL3 := (NOT PrintToExcel AND NOT AdviceOrderFound);

                                  TempAdviceOrderLine.RESET;
                                  ShowBL4 := ((TempAdviceOrderLine.COUNT = 0) AND (NOT PrintToExcel));
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Project No.,Element,Item No.,Extension Contract;
               DataItemLink=Project No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100525003;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               TempAdviceOrderLine.RESET;
                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempAdviceOrderLine.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ProjElement@1100525000 : Record 11012010;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempAdviceOrderLine.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempAdviceOrderLine.NEXT;


                                  ClearVariables;
                                  AdviceOrderFound := GetAdviceOrder(TempAdviceOrderLine."Project No.",TempAdviceOrderLine.Element,TempAdviceOrderLine."Item No.",
                                                      GAdvice,GProcessed,GReceived,GStatus,GPurchCode,GAskDate,
                                                      GPromDate, GQuantArtDagb, GStockQuant, GToReceive, GTransAct, GLineNo,TRUE,
                                                      TempAdviceOrderLine.Description);
                                  ElementDesc := GetElementDesc(TempAdviceOrderLine."Project No.",TempAdviceOrderLine.Element);

                                  CLEAR(StartDate);
                                  IF TempAdviceOrderLine.Element <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF ProjElement.GET(TempAdviceOrderLine."Project No.",TempAdviceOrderLine.Element) THEN
                                      IF ProjElement."Starting Date" <> 0D THEN
                                        StartDate := ProjElement."Starting Date";
                                  END;

                                  GProcessed1 := GProcessed;

                                  IF (GStatus = 'Afgehandeld') AND (GTransAct = 'Voorraad') THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (GQuantArtDagb <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                      GStockQuant := GQuantArtDagb;
                                      GProcessed1 := GProcessed - GQuantArtDagb;
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      GStockQuant := 0;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF (GStatus = 'Afgehandeld') AND (GTransAct = 'Inkoop') THEN BEGIN
                                    IF JobStockSpec(TempAdviceOrderLine."Item No.", Job."No.", TempAdviceOrderLine.Element) <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                      GProcessed1 := JobStockSpec(TempAdviceOrderLine."Item No.", Job."No.", TempAdviceOrderLine.Element);
                                      GStockQuant := GProcessed - GProcessed1;
                                    END ELSE
                                      GProcessed1 := GProcessed - GStockQuant;
                                  END;

                                  //FROM SECTION

                                  IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 21 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := Matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := Job."No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := TempAdviceOrderLine.Element;
                                    IF StartDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := StartDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := ElementDesc;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := TempAdviceOrderLine."Item No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := TempAdviceOrderLine.Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := TempAdviceOrderLine."Extension Contract";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := FORMAT(TempAdviceOrderLine."Quantity (Budget)");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := FORMAT(GAdviceBl);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := FORMAT(GAdvice);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := FORMAT(GProcessed);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := FORMAT(GStatus);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := FORMAT(GQuantArtDagb);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[14]).Value := FORMAT(GTransAct);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[15]).Value := FORMAT(GPurchCode);
                                    IF GAskDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := GAskDate;
                                    IF GPromDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := GPromDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := FORMAT(GStockQuant);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := FORMAT(GProcessed1);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := FORMAT(
                                      JobStock(TempAdviceOrderLine."Item No.", Job."No.", TempAdviceOrderLine.Element));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Value := FORMAT(
                                      JobStockDelivery(TempAdviceOrderLine."Item No.", Job."No.", TempAdviceOrderLine.Element));
                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END;
                                  //CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(NOT PrintToExcel);

                                  TempAdviceOrderLine.RESET;
                                  ShowInt2 := ((TempAdviceOrderLine.COUNT <> 0) AND (NOT PrintToExcel));
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525025;2;Column;IntegerGROUP       ;

               SourceExpr=JobStockDelivery(TempAdviceOrderLine."Item No.", Job."No.", TempAdviceOrderLine.Element) }

    { 1100525004;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table39;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Document Type,Job No.,Extension Contract,Cost Type,Shortcut Dimension 2 Code,Order Date)
                                 WHERE(Document Type=CONST(Order));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               SETFILTER(Element,"Budget Line".GETFILTER(Element));
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lDec@1100525008 : Decimal;
                                  lInt@1100525007 : Integer;
                                  lText@1100525006 : Text[30];
                                  lCode@1100525005 : Code[10];
                                  lDate@1100525004 : Date;
                                  lLineNo@1100525003 : Integer;
                                  AdviceOrderLine@1100525002 : Record 11012055;
                                  PurchLine@1100525001 : Record 39;
                                  ProjElement@1100525000 : Record 11012010;
                                BEGIN

                                  ClearVariables;

                                  AdviceOrderFound := GetAdviceOrder(Job."No.",Element,"Item No.",lDec,lDec,lDec,lText,lCode,lDate,lDate,lDec,
                                                                     lDec,lDec,lText,lLineNo,TRUE, Description);

                                  IF AdviceOrderFound THEN CurrReport.SKIP;
                                  ElementDesc := GetElementDesc(Job."No.",Element);

                                  IF (GTransAct = 'Inkoop') AND (GLineNo <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                    //Bepalen inkooporder regel
                                    IF AdviceOrderLine.GET(AdviceOrderLine."Record Type"::Project,Job."No.",'',GLineNo) THEN BEGIN
                                      PurchLine.SETRANGE("Job No.",Job."No.");
                                      PurchLine.SETRANGE("Purchase Route Reference",AdviceOrderLine."Purchase Route Reference");
                                      IF PurchLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                        GStockQuant := PurchLine."Qty. to Receive";
                                        GProcessed :=  AdviceOrderLine."Quantity (Processed)";
                                      END;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  CLEAR(StartDate);
                                  IF Element <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF ProjElement.GET(Job."No.",Element) THEN
                                      IF ProjElement."Starting Date" <> 0D THEN
                                        StartDate := ProjElement."Starting Date";
                                  END;

                                  IF (GStatus = 'Afgehandeld') AND (GTransAct = 'Voorraad') THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (GQuantArtDagb <> 0) THEN
                                      GStockQuant := GQuantArtDagb
                                    ELSE
                                      GStockQuant := 0;
                                  END;

                                  //FROM SECTION

                                  IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 20 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := Matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := Job."No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := Element;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := ElementDesc;
                                    IF StartDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := StartDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := "Item No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := Description;

                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := FORMAT(Quantity);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[14]).Value := 'Inkoop';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[15]).Value := "Document No.";
                                    IF "Requested Receipt Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := "Requested Receipt Date";
                                    IF "Promised Receipt Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := "Expected Receipt Date";
                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END;

                                  ShowPurchLine2 := (NOT PrintToExcel);
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Job No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100525026;2;Column;PurchaseLineGROUP  ;
               SourceExpr='PurchaseLine' }

    { 1100525005;1;DataItem;JobInventory     ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               TempJobInventory.RESET;
                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempJobInventory.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ProjElement@1100525000 : Record 11012010;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempJobInventory.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempJobInventory.NEXT;
                                  ClearVariables;

                                  TempJobInventory.CALCFIELDS("Inventory Quantity");

                                  ElementDesc := GetElementDesc(TempJobInventory."Project No.", TempJobInventory.Element);

                                  CLEAR(StartDate);
                                  IF TempJobInventory.Element <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF ProjElement.GET(TempJobInventory."Project No.", TempJobInventory.Element) THEN
                                      IF ProjElement."Starting Date" <> 0D THEN
                                        StartDate := ProjElement."Starting Date";
                                  END;

                                  IF (GStatus = 'Afgehandeld') AND (GTransAct = 'Voorraad') THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (GQuantArtDagb <> 0) THEN
                                      GStockQuant := GQuantArtDagb
                                    ELSE
                                      GStockQuant := 0;
                                  END;

                                  CLEAR(GQuantArtDagb);

                                  //FROM SECTION

                                  IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 21 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := Matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := Job."No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := TempJobInventory.Element;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := ElementDesc;
                                    IF StartDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := StartDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := TempJobInventory."Item No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := TempJobInventory.Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := '1';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := JobStock(TempAdviceOrderLine."Item No.", Job."No.", TempAdviceOrderLine.Element);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Value := JobStockDelivery(TempAdviceOrderLine."Item No.", Job."No.", TempAdviceOrderLine.Element);
                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END;

                                  //CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(NOT PrintToExcel);
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525056;2;Column;JobInventoryGROUP  ;
               SourceExpr='JobInventory' }

    { 1100525006;2;Column;TempJobInventoryElement_JobInventory;
               SourceExpr=TempJobInventory.Element }

    PROCEDURE ClearVariables@1000000048();
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(GAdvice);
      CLEAR(GProcessed);
      CLEAR(GProcessed1);
      CLEAR(GReceived);
      CLEAR(GStatus);
      CLEAR(GPurchCode);
      CLEAR(GAskDate);
      CLEAR(GPromDate);
      CLEAR(GQuantArtDagb);
      CLEAR(GAdviceBl);
      CLEAR(GStockQuant);
      CLEAR(GToReceive);
      CLEAR(ElementDesc);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetAdviceOrder@1000000024(ProjectNo@1000000001 : Code[20];ElementCde@1000000002 : Code[20];ItemNo@1000000003 : Code[20];VAR Advice@1000000004 : Decimal;VAR Processed@1000000005 : Decimal;VAR Received@1000000006 : Decimal;VAR Status@1000000007 : Text[50];VAR PurchCode@1000000009 : Code[20];VAR AskDate@1000000011 : Date;VAR PromDate@1000000012 : Date;VAR QuantArtDagb@1000000013 : Decimal;VAR StockQuant@1000000015 : Decimal;VAR ToReceive@1000000016 : Decimal;VAR Transact@1000000017 : Text[50];VAR AdviceOrderLineNo@1000000019 : Integer;DeleteBl@1000000018 : Boolean;Description@1000000020 : Text[50]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      AdviceOrder@1000000000 : Record 11012055;
      PurchLine@1000000008 : Record 39;
      ItemJournlLine@1000000010 : Record 83;
      FromText@1000000014 : TextConst;
      ToText@1000000021 : TextConst;
    BEGIN
      AdviceOrder.SETRANGE("Record Type",AdviceOrder."Record Type"::Project);
      AdviceOrder.SETRANGE("Project No.",ProjectNo);
      AdviceOrder.SETRANGE(Element,ElementCde);

      IF ItemNo <> '' THEN
        AdviceOrder.SETRANGE("Item No."  ,ItemNo)
      ELSE
        AdviceOrder.SETRANGE( Description, Description);

      IF AdviceOrder.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        Advice := AdviceOrder."Quantity (Advice)";
        Processed := AdviceOrder."Quantity (Processed)";
        Received := AdviceOrder.ReceivedPurchaseQuantity(COMPANYNAME);
        Status := FORMAT(AdviceOrder."Process Status");
        Transact := FORMAT(AdviceOrder.Transaction);
        AskDate := AdviceOrder."Receipt Date";
        AdviceOrderLineNo := AdviceOrder."Line No.";

        //Temprecordsfilteren en verwijderen
        IF NOT DeleteBl THEN BEGIN
          TempAdviceOrderLine.RESET;
          TempAdviceOrderLine.SETRANGE("Record Type",TempAdviceOrderLine."Record Type"::Project);
          TempAdviceOrderLine.SETRANGE("Project No.",AdviceOrder."Project No.");
          TempAdviceOrderLine.SETRANGE(Element,AdviceOrder.Element);
          TempAdviceOrderLine.SETRANGE("Item No.",AdviceOrder."Item No.");
          IF TempAdviceOrderLine.FINDFIRST THEN
            TempAdviceOrderLine.DELETE;
        END;

        IF AdviceOrder."Purchase Route Reference" <> '' THEN BEGIN
          PurchLine.SETRANGE("Purchase Route Reference",AdviceOrder."Purchase Route Reference");
          IF PurchLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            PurchCode := PurchLine."Document No.";
            AskDate := PurchLine."Requested Receipt Date";
            PromDate := PurchLine."Expected Receipt Date";
            StockQuant := PurchLine."Qty. Received (Base)"; //"Quantity (Base)";  29-10-2010
            //Processed := PurchLine."Qty. Received (Base)";
            Processed := PurchLine."Quantity (Base)";
          END;
        END;
        ItemJournlLine.SETRANGE("Job No.",ProjectNo);
        ItemJournlLine.SETRANGE(Element,ElementCde);
        ItemJournlLine.SETRANGE("Item No.",ItemNo);
        IF ItemJournlLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          QuantArtDagb := ItemJournlLine.Quantity;
        END;
       END ELSE
        EXIT(FALSE);

      TempJobInventory.RESET;
      TempJobInventory.SETRANGE("Project No.",ProjectNo);
      TempJobInventory.SETRANGE(Element,ElementCde);
      IF ItemNo <> '' THEN
        TempJobInventory.SETRANGE("Item No.",ItemNo)
      ELSE BEGIN
        Description := CONVERTSTR(Description, FromText, ToText);
        TempJobInventory.SETFILTER( Description, '@' + Description);
      END;

      IF TempJobInventory.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          TempJobInventory.CALCFIELDS("Inventory Quantity");
          StockQuant -= TempJobInventory.Quantity;
        UNTIL TempJobInventory.NEXT = 0;
        TempJobInventory.DELETEALL;
      END;

      EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetElementDesc@1000000006(ProjectNo@1000000000 : Code[20];ElementCde@1000000001 : Code[20]) : Text[50];
    VAR
      ProjElement@1000000002 : Record 11012010;
    BEGIN
      IF ProjElement.GET(ProjectNo,ElementCde) THEN
        EXIT(ProjElement.Description)
      ELSE
        EXIT('');
    END;

    PROCEDURE Matrix@1100525000(ColNo@1100525000 : Integer;RowNo@1100525001 : Integer) : Text[30];
    VAR
      TempExcelBuffer@1100525002 : TEMPORARY Record 370;
    BEGIN
      TempExcelBuffer.VALIDATE("Column No.",ColNo);
      TempExcelBuffer.VALIDATE("Row No.",RowNo);
      EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1%2',TempExcelBuffer.xlColID,TempExcelBuffer.xlRowID));
    END;

    PROCEDURE HideSheets@1000000000();
    BEGIN
      //Basis sheets verbergen
      xlSheet := xlApp.Worksheets.Item('Sheet1');
      xlSheet.Select;
      xlSheet.Visible(2);
      xlSheet := xlApp.Worksheets.Item('Sheet2');
      xlSheet.Select;
      xlSheet.Visible(2);
      xlSheet := xlApp.Worksheets.Item('Sheet3');
      xlSheet.Select;
      xlSheet.Visible(2);
    END;

    PROCEDURE JobStock@1000000002(ItemNo@1000000000 : Code[20];JobNo@1000000001 : Code[20];ElementNo@1000000003 : Code[10]) Qty : Decimal;
    VAR
      ProjectInventoryDelivery@1000000002 : Record 11012670;
    BEGIN
      ProjectInventoryDelivery.SETRANGE("Project No.", JobNo    );
      ProjectInventoryDelivery.SETRANGE("Item No."   , ItemNo   );
      ProjectInventoryDelivery.SETRANGE( Element     , ElementNo);
      IF NOT ProjectInventoryDelivery.FINDSET(FALSE, FALSE) THEN
        EXIT(0)
      ELSE BEGIN
        REPEAT
          ProjectInventoryDelivery.CALCFIELDS("Inventory Quantity");
          Qty += ProjectInventoryDelivery.Quantity;
        UNTIL ProjectInventoryDelivery.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      EXIT(Qty);
    END;

    PROCEDURE JobStockDelivery@1000000004(ItemNo@1000000003 : Code[20];JobNo@1000000002 : Code[20];ElementNo@1000000001 : Code[10]) Qty : Decimal;
    VAR
      ProjInventEntry@1000000000 : Record 11012670;
    BEGIN
      ProjInventEntry.SETRANGE("Project No.", JobNo);
      ProjInventEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.", ItemNo);
      ProjInventEntry.SETRANGE(Element,ElementNo);
      ProjInventEntry.SETRANGE("Entry Type", ProjInventEntry."Entry Type"::Delivery);
      IF NOT ProjInventEntry.FINDSET THEN
        EXIT(0)
      ELSE BEGIN
        REPEAT
          Qty += ProjInventEntry.Quantity;
        UNTIL ProjInventEntry.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE JobStockSpec@1000000001(ItemNo@1000000000 : Code[20];JobNo@1000000001 : Code[20];ElementNo@1000000003 : Code[10]) Qty : Decimal;
    VAR
      ProjectInventoryDelivery@1000000002 : Record 11012670;
    BEGIN
      ProjectInventoryDelivery.SETRANGE("Project No.", JobNo    );
      ProjectInventoryDelivery.SETRANGE("Item No."   , ItemNo   );
      ProjectInventoryDelivery.SETRANGE( Element     , ElementNo);
      IF NOT ProjectInventoryDelivery.FINDSET(FALSE, FALSE) THEN
        EXIT(0)
      ELSE BEGIN
        REPEAT
          ProjectInventoryDelivery.CALCFIELDS("Inventory Quantity");
          IF ProjectInventoryDelivery.Quantity > 0 THEN
            Qty += ProjectInventoryDelivery.Quantity;
        UNTIL ProjectInventoryDelivery.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      EXIT(Qty);
    END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
